angular.module('ng').run(['$rootScope', function ($rootScope) {
    $rootScope.$safeApply = function (fn) {
        try {
            var phase = (this.$root) ? this.$root.$$phase : null;
            if (phase == '$apply' || phase == '$digest') {
                if (fn && (typeof(fn) === 'function')) {
                    this.$eval(fn);
                }
            } else {
                this.$apply(fn);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error(e);
        }
    };
}]);

        try {
            var phase = (this.$root) ? this.$root.$$phase : null;
            if (phase == '$apply' || phase == '$digest') {

                    this.$eval(fn);

angular.module('ng').run(['$rootScope', function ($rootScope) {
    $rootScope.$safeApply = function (fn) {
        try {
            var phase = (this.$root) ? this.$root.$$phase : null;
            if (phase == '$apply' || phase == '$digest') {
                if (fn && (typeof(fn) === 'function')) {
                    this.$eval(fn);
                }
            } else {
                this.$apply(fn);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error(e);
        }
    };
}]);
